msg:The stay at the hotel was good. The hotel facilities are old but in good shape. The location is perfect for people who cross to and from HK. There are a lot of good places nearby to enjoy a good time, dinner, and shopping. Also, the hotel offers free parking. The amenities are good quality and plenty of them, which is very weird in those times of savings from big Hotel chains. Therefore I enjoy the amenities of this hotel. 
The only annoying thing was the cleaning service crew. They started to pressure me at 11 AM (checkout is at 12 pm), but they knocked on the door insistently, and after I went out, somebody reached me to ask me if the room was empty. It is a sincerely very uncomfortable sense. I prefer another hotel that respects those details.
Referring to shower, the curtain was dirty and old, need to pay more attention to cleaning process.

msg:We stayed here for two nights. The hotel location is close to the railway station and KK100 mall, and MixC mall. The staff was friendly, kind, and pleasant. The breakfast selection is fantastic. There are different types of cuisine that you can try. Using the metro station, you can reach the hotel on line 1, exit E1 or E2. The room is excellent; the bathtub is awesome. There is a rooftop bar on the 31st floor. You can enjoy your drinks and food by looking at the fantastic view of Shenzhen and Hongkong. 
The pool is clean, and so does the gym. There are saunas and a jacuzzi as well. 
I will surely come back to this hotel. 
Recommended.

The hotel will provide a robot to deliver it directly to the room, which is very suitable for patients with "cancer dependence". The hotel's epidemic prevention is also very good. No matter which door you come in from, there will be personnel on duty to guard you, and you will be asked to show your health code.
